<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въезд</a> (8448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезжать.html>въезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vʺjezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въезд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vʺjezd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въе́зда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въе́зды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезд.html>въе́здов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>entry, entrance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of entering, especially when using any means of transportation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>entry, entrance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">doorway that provides a means of entering a building</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***въезжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:въезжать.html>въезжа́ть</a> (11141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезжать.html>въезжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vʺjezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въехать.html>въе́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enter (by vehicle), to go in(to) (by vehicle)</li>
<li>to move into (e.g. a new house)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand, to get</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:въесться.html>въе́сться</a> (20068)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въесться.html>въе́сться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vʺjéstʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">въеда́ться</b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<ol><li>to penetrate into, to saturate, to impregnate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to penetrate deeply, to pierce</li></ol>

***въехать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:въехать.html>въе́хать</a> (5507)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въехать.html>въе́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vʺjéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:въезжать.html>въезжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enter (by vehicle), to ride in, to drive in, to go in(to) (by vehicle)</li>
<li>to move into (e.g. a new house)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand, to get</li></ol>

***вы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> (25)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vy</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vy</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>you <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural or formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The personal pronoun <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a></span> is comparable to French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">vous</i>, German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sie</i>, Spanish <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">usted</i>, and is used not only in the plural sense, but also as the formal singular. The formal <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a></span> is appropriate with strangers, business contacts, neighbors, and friends. (The informal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> should only be used with family and friends. Even then, a speaker may suddenly switch to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a></span> in order to broach an especially serious topic, or to indicate displeasure or anger.) For more information, see Appendix:Russian pronouns
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ваш</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vaš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбегать.html>выбега́ть</a> (8297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбегать.html>выбега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vybegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбежать.html>вы́бежать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run out (outside)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полчаса.html>полчаса́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбегать.html>выбега́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:калитка.html>кали́тке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посмотреть.html>посмотре́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приехать.html>прие́хал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:папа.html>па́па</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Káždyje polčasá on <b>vybegál</b> k kalítke posmotrétʹ, ne prijéxal li papa.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Every half hour he ran to the gate to see if dad had arrived.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***выбивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a> (8891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vybivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat out, to knock out, to dislodge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́теля</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> protívnika / neprijátelja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dislodge the enemy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оконный.html>око́нное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> okónnoje stekló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smash a pane</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седло.html>седла́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> iz sedlá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unseat, to unhorse, to cut the ground (out) from under, to throw someone from balance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пыль.html>пыль</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> чего́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> pylʹ (iz čevó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat the dust out of something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:медаль.html>меда́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> medálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike a medal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:барабанный.html>бараба́нную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дробь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> barabánnuju drobʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat a tattoo</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колея.html>колеи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> kovó-libo iz koleí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unsettle someone, to upset someone's routine</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дурь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>головы́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹ</b> durʹ iz golový</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock the nonsense out of someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбиваться.html>выбива́ться</a> (13589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vybivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиваться.html>выбива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vybivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиться.html>вы́биться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get out, to break loose (from), to show (from under), to work loose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиваться.html>выбива́ются</a></b> и́з-под <a href = vnd.unilang:шляпа.html>шля́пы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nejó vólosy <b>vybivájutsja</b> íz-pod šljápy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">her hair is coming out from under the hat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиваться.html>выбива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колея.html>колеи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹsja</b> iz koleí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go off the rails (figuratively)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиваться.html>выбива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹsja</b> iz sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to become completely exhausted</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиваться.html>выбива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vybivátʹsja</b> v ljúdi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get on in the world</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vybivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***выбирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбирать.html>выбира́ть</a> (1948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбирать.html>выбира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vybirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбрать.html>вы́брать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to choose, to select, to pick out</li>
<li>to elect</li>
<li>to take everything out</li>
<li>to haul in (<i>net</i>), to pull up (<i>anchor</i>)</li>
<li>to find (<i>free time, etc.</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избирать.html>избира́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отбирать.html>отбира́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отсе́ивать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otséivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голосовать.html>голосова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">golosovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:избирать.html>избира́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izvlekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изымать.html>изыма́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izymátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<ol><li>to get out

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбирать.html>выбира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vybirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***выбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a> (3742)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výbitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбивать.html>выбива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat out, to knock out, to dislodge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́теля</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> protívnika / neprijátelja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dislodge the enemy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оконный.html>око́нное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> okónnoje stekló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to smash a pane</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седло.html>седла́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> iz sedlá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unseat, to unhorse, to cut the ground (out) from under, to throw someone from balance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пыль.html>пыль</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> чего́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> pylʹ (iz čevó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat the dust out of something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:медаль.html>меда́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> medálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike a medal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:барабанный.html>бараба́нную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дробь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> barabánnuju drobʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat a tattoo</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колея.html>колеи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> kovó-libo iz koleí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unsettle someone, to upset someone's routine</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дурь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>головы́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹ</b> durʹ iz golový</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock the nonsense out of someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбиться.html>вы́биться</a> (11526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиться.html>вы́биться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výbitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиваться.html>выбива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get out, to break loose (from), to show (from under), to work loose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиться.html>вы́бились</a></b> и́з-под <a href = vnd.unilang:шляпа.html>шля́пы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nejó vólosy <b>výbilisʹ</b> íz-pod šljápy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">her hair came out from under the hat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиться.html>вы́биться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колея.html>колеи́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹsja</b> iz koleí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go off the rails (figuratively)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиться.html>вы́биться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹsja</b> iz sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to become completely exhausted</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбиться.html>вы́биться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výbitʹsja</b> v ljúdi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get on in the world</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбить.html>вы́бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбоина.html>вы́боина</a> (22197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбоина.html>вы́боина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výboina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбоина.html>вы́боины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбоина.html>вы́боины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбоина.html>вы́боин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pothole
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>Еду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбоина.html>вы́боинам</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выбоина.html>вы́боин</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выехать.html>вы́еду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jedu ja po <b>výboinam</b>, iz <b>výboin</b> ne výjedu ja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I am driving along potholes, never going to drive out of them. (<i>A pun tongue-twister, intended to sound obscene if mispronounced.</i>)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбросить.html>вы́бросить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výbrositʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбрасывать.html>выбра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vybrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбросить.html>вы́бросить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw away <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">discard or dispose of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to emit, to eject</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбрасываться.html>выбра́сываться</a> (23606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбрасывать.html>выбра́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vybrásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбрасываться.html>выбра́сываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vybrásyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выброситься.html>вы́броситься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jump down <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to throw oneself <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to be thrown <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to erupt <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of jets of flame, streams of water, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выбрасывать.html>выбра́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vybrásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
